                            teardown.throw(exception)[90m[39;49;00m
                        [94mexcept[39;49;00m [96mRuntimeError[39;49;00m [94mas[39;49;00m re:[90m[39;49;00m
                            [90m# StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError[39;49;00m[90m[39;49;00m

                                [96misinstance[39;49;00m(exception, [96mStopIteration[39;49;00m)[90m[39;49;00m

                    [94mcontinue[39;49;00m[90m[39;49;00m
                [94mexcept[39;49;00m [96mBaseException[39;49;00m [94mas[39;49;00m e:[90m[39;49;00m
                    exception = e[90m[39;49;00m
                    [94mcontinue[39;49;00m[90m[39;49;00m
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, [33m"[39;49;00m[33mhas second yield[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[90m[39;49;00m
    [90m[39;49;00m
        [94mif[39;49;00m exception [95mis[39;49;00m [95mnot[39;49;00m [94mNone[39;49;00m:[90m[39;49;00m
